V<br \/>= 0,1 mol\/L . 0,2 L<br \/>= 0,02 mol<br \/><br \/>Mencari mol OH- yang ditambahkan :<br \/>pOH :<br \/>= 14 - pH<br \/>=14 - 13<br \/>= 1<br \/><br \/>[OH-] :<br \/>- log [OH-] = pOH<br \/>- log [OH-] = 1<br \/>- log [OH-] = - log 10^-1<br \/>[OH-] = 10^-1<br \/><br \/>mol OH- :<br \/>= M .
